Ncmec Reports Definition
NCMEC Cybertips: NCMEC cybertip reports associated to the account of the sender.
CyberTip ID: Unique identifier associated with the cybertip.
Time: Date and time the NCMEC cybertip was sent.
Responsible Id: Identification number of the sender's Facebook account associated with the NCMEC cybertip report.
- Details: Text and/or media associated with the cybertip
- Text and/or Media ID: The unique system-generated ID associated with the content.
- Upload Time: Date and timestamp the account holder uploaded the content.
- User Generated Filename: Name of the media file when the account holder uploaded the media to the platform.
- Upload IP: IP address captured at the time the account holder uploaded the media.
- NCMEC File ID: File ID provided by NCMEC associated with the cybertip.
- Human Reviewed: If the content was manually reviewed.
- Yes: Content in the file were viewed by an employee or contractor at Meta concurrently with or immediately before the file was submitted to NCMEC.
- No: Historically at least one employee or contractor at Meta viewed a file whose hash matched the hash of the reported content and determined it contained apparent child pornography.
Meta Platforms Business Record Page 2
- Recipients: The account holder that received the content.
- Media: The bytes associated with the uploaded media.
- PhotoDNA Hash: The unique system-generated ID signature/hash of the uploaded media.
- Caption: Caption posted with the media.
- Sharepoint: Sharepoint is the location where the content was shared within the platform.
- Metadata: Metadata associated with media
- Messages: Up to 3 messages above and below the reported content.
- Reported Text (alternative to Media associated with cybertip): Text only content that has been reported associated with the cybertip
- Industry CSAM Classification: The industry CSAM classification media depictions.
- NCMEC Defined Product Annotations: File depiction annotation associated with the cybertip.

Logins Definition
Logins: Information collected at the time the account was logged into.
Ip Address: IP Address: IP address and source port/port number associated with the login. Source port/ port numbers are provided when available. If available, it is located at the end of the IP address, after the colon.
Time: Date and timestamp of the login.
Shared Access: The authorized account holder associated with the login.

Photos Definition
Photos: Information about the photos uploaded to the account.
ID: Unique system generated Identifier of the image.
Taken: Date and timestamp the image was uploaded.
Status: Status is whether the image can be viewed.
URL: Link to the photo.
Source: Refers to the device through which the photo was taken.
Filter: Displays the filter used on the image.
Meta Platforms Business Record Page 213
Is Published: Indicates if the image is currently on the profile.
Shared to Platform: Indicates if the photo was shared to a different platform (true) or only posted to IG (false).
Like Count: The number of likes the content has.
Carousel ID: The unique system-generated ID that is created when a post contains more than one media.
Upload IP: IP address and source port/port numbers associated with the uploaded image. Source port/ port numbers are provided when available. If available, it is located at the end of the IP address, after the colon.
Owner: Owner of the account.
Author: The authorized account holder who uploaded the photo.
Bytes: Link to the media.
Caption: Caption associated with the photo.
Owner: The account that shared the caption.
Author: The authorized account holder that posted the caption.
ID: Unique system generated identifier for the caption.
Date Created: Date / timestamp of when the caption was posted.
Text: User generated text.
Deleted by Instagram: Any photo that Instagram removed from the platform for violating the terms of service.
Privacy Setting: Displays current privacy settings for content.
- Public: The privacy setting of the content is Public.
- Private: The privacy setting of the content is Private.
- Close Friends: The privacy setting of the content is only viewable to Close Friends.
Like Count: The number of likes the content has.

No responsive records located
Unified Messages Definition
Unified Messages: Private communication between account holders.
Thread: Unique identifier associated with conversation thread.
Current Participants: Account holders included in conversation thread.
Owner: Owner of the account.
Author: The authorized account holder that sent the message on behalf of the owner.
Sent: Date and time of communication sent.
Removed by Sender: Indicates that the communication has been removed by the sender.
Call Record: Indicates a call was made through conversation thread.
Type: Indicates the method in which a call was placed.
Missed: Indicates if the call was missed.
Duration: Length of the call (in seconds).
Thread Name: Name given to the chat thread by the group admin.
Encrypted Calls: Calls that were encrypted.
Product Type: Appears for Instagram Direct Messaging, specifically for Instagram messenger Videos and Photos which may be ephemeral or not. There are three possible values which may surface, VIEW_ONCE, REPLAYABLE and PERMANENT.
Attachments: Files associated with the communication.
Type: Description of the type of attachment.
Size: The size of the file sent.
URL: URL of the content.
Product Type: The description of the attachment product type.
Meta Platforms Business Record Page 221
Permanent: The media does not expire in the account holder’s unified thread.
Replayable: The viewer has the ability to replay the media once.
View Once: The media disappears after the recipient views it.
Body: Text of communication, or description of content type sent.
Attachments: Files associated with the communication.
Type: Description of what type of attachment.
Size: The size of the file sent.
URL: URL of the content.
Past Participants: Lists the account holders that have previously been subscribed to the conversation thread.
Subscription Event: Indicates an update to a participant's subscription to the conversation thread.
Type: Indicates action associated with the participant.
Users: the account holders impacted by the subscription update.
Share: Items shared into the communication thread between account holders.
Date Created: Date and time associated with the share.
Text: Content of the share.
URL: URL of the content.
AI: Message threads that include content generated by Generative AI.
True= AI content is included in the message thread.
False= AI content is not included in the message thread.
AI Searches: A specific search made by the account holder that generates AI stickers within a chat.
Read Receipts: A user-enabled setting that indicates whether the account holder’s read receipts will be automatically displayed to other users.
Meta Platforms Business Record Page 222
Enabled: The thread level setting for when read receipts are turned on. This is the default setting.
Disabled: The thread level setting for when read receipts are turned off.

Facebook retains the author, but NOT the recipient(s), of individual messages for Messenger threads. Facebook also retains the following information for Messenger threads:
(1) Current Thread Participants – a list of all accounts subscribed to a thread at the time Facebook retrieved the records;
(2) Past Thread Participants – a list of all accounts previously (but not currently) subscribed to a thread at any time before the records were retrieved; and
(3) Subscription Event – a log of an account subscribing to (joining) or unsubscribing from (leaving) a thread during the date range covered by the production. Subscription events that fall outside of the date range covered by the production are not included.
Likes Definition
Likes: Media the account holder liked.
ID: Unique system generated identifier of the action.
Taken: Date and timestamp of when the media was uploaded to IG.
Status: The current status of the media on the account.
Liked Post Owner Vanity: Username of the post owner that the account holder liked.
Like Timestamp: Date and time the account holder liked the post.
URL: The link to the media.
Source: Where the media is uploaded from
Meta Platforms Business Record Page 251
Filter: The filter used on the media.
Is Published: Indicates if the media is currently on the profile.
Shared to Platform: Indicates if the media was shared to a different platform (true) or only posted to IG (false).
Upload IP: IP address captured at the time when the liked post is uploaded
Cross Post ID: The unique system-generated ID of the media that has been shared from Instagram to Facebook.
Owner: Owner of the account.
Author: The authorized account holder who liked the media.

Comment Likes Definition
Comment Likes displays the comment liked by the account holder
Like timestamp: date and timestamp the account holder liked the comment
Comment Author Vanity: Account holder that made the comment
Post URL of Comment liked: URL of the comment liked
Comment Likes
No responsive records located
Reported Conversations Definition
Reported Conversations: Private messages reported to Meta.
Reported Conversation ID: Unique identifier associated with the conversation thread.
Participants: Account holders participating in the conversation.
Meta Platforms Business Record Page 333
Reporter: Account holder who reported the conversation.
Time Reported: Date and timestamp the conversation was reported.
Sender: Account holder or authorized account holder who sent the messages.
Owner: Owner of the account.
Sent: Date and time message was sent.
Message: Body of message.
Attachments: Attachments associated with the reported content.
Type: Type of attachment.
URL: Link associated with attachment.
Photo ID: Unique system generated identifier associated with image.
Reported Conversations
No responsive records located
Reported Disappearing Messages Definition
Reported Disappearing Messages: Private disappearing messages reported to Meta.
Participants: Account holders participating in the disappearing messages conversation.
Reporter: Account holder who reported the disappearing message(s).
Time Reported: Date and timestamp the conversation was reported.
Disappearing Messages Thread ID: Unique system generated identifier of the thread with set duration.
Sender: Account holder or authorized account holder who sent the disappearing messages.
Owner: Owner of the account.
Sent: Date and time the reported disappearing messages were sent.
Message: Body of the reported disappearing messages.
Attachments: Attachments associated with the reported disappearing message(s).
Meta Platforms Business Record Page 334
Type: Type of attachment.
URL: Link associated with attachment.
Photo ID: Unique system generated identifier associated with the image.
Reported Disappearing Messages
No responsive records located
Archived Stories Definition
Archived Stories: Displays media the user posted to their profile story that have been archived.
Story ID: Unique system generated identifier of the story.
Time: Timestamp is the date and time the media was uploaded.
Owner: Owner of the account.
Author: The authorized account holder who uploaded the story.
Bytes: Link to the media.
Privacy Setting: Displays current privacy settings for content.
- Public: The privacy setting of the content is Public.
- Private: The privacy setting of the content is Private.
- Close Friends: The privacy setting of the content is only viewable to Close Friends.
AI: Identifies if the content was created using Generative AI.
- True: Content was created using Generative AI.
- False: Content was not created using Generative AI.
AI Searches: Searches made by the account holder that generate AI stickers within a story.
Archived Stories
Story Id
18067427045073983
Time
2025-06-06 14:50:28 UTC
Privacy Setting
PRIVATE
Meta Platforms Business Record Page 335
Linked Media File:
linked_media/archived_stories_18067427045073983.mp4

evairoucr7 (Instagram: 14350238324)
AI

False
Encrypted Groups Info Definition
Encrypted Groups Info: Information on the encrypted group messages that the account holder owns or participates in.
Administrators: Account holders involved in conversation thread.
Creation time: Displays time of creation of group.
Creator: Displays creator name.
ID: Unique ID associated with the group.
Participants: Account holders who were included in the group.
Size: Size of the group (i.e. number of participants).
Subject: Name of the group.
Subject Owner: Account holder who named the group.
Subject Time: Date and timestamp when the group was named.
Encrypted Groups Info
No responsive records located
Threads Profile Picture Definition
Threads Profile Picture: Uploaded profile photo of the Threads account at the time of data production.
Photo ID: The unique system-generated ID associated with the photo.
Threads Profile Picture
No responsive records located
Threads Following Definition
Threads Following:
Following: Threads Accounts that the account holder is following at the time of data production.
Timestamp: The date and time when the account holder followed other Threads accounts.
Threads Following
Meta Platforms Business Record Page 336
No responsive records located
Threads Followers Definition
Threads Followers:
Follower: Threads accounts that follow the account holder at the time of data production.
Timestamp: The date and time when Threads accounts followed the account holder.
Threads Followers
No responsive records located
Threads Liked Posts Definition
Threads Liked Posts:
Timestamp: The time and date the account holder liked a Threads post.
Post Author Vanity: Author of the Threads Post.
Post URL of Like Post: URL link of the Threads Post.
Threads Liked Posts
No responsive records located
Threads Registration Date Definition
Threads Registration Date: The date and time when the account holder registered an account on the Threads App.
Threads Registration Date
Unknown
Threads Account Searches Definition
Threads Account Searches:
Account: Threads Accounts searched and selected by the account holder.
Timestamp: The date and time when the account holder searched and selected a Threads account.
Threads Account Searches
No responsive records located
Threads Keyword Searches Definition
Keywords: Words searched by the account holder.
Timestamp: The date and time when the account holder searched a word
Threads Keyword Searches
No responsive records located
Threads Muted Users Definition
Threads Muted Users:
Muted User: The Threads account that has been muted by the account holder.
Meta Platforms Business Record Page 337
Timestamp: The date and time the Threads account was muted by the account holder.
Threads Muted Users
No responsive records located
Threads Incoming Follow Requests Definition
Threads Incoming Follow Requests:
Incoming Follow Requests: Threads account follow requests received that have not been confirmed or deleted by the account holder.
Timestamp: The date and time that the Threads account follow request was received.
Threads Incoming Follow Requests
No responsive records located
Threads Posts And Replies Definition
Threads Posts and Replies: Posts and replies the account holder made in the Threads App.
- Post Author ID: The unique system-generated ID of the author who created a Threads post or reply.
- Post Content ID: The unique system-generated ID of the Threads post or reply content.
- Timestamp: Date and timestamp of when the author made the Threads post or reply.
- Post Setting: Setting of who can reply to the Threads post or reply. (Anyone, Profiles you follow, Mentioned only)
- Reply to Author: The unique system-generated author ID for the Threads post or reply that the account holder replied to.
- Reply to (Post) ID: The unique system-generated ID of the Threads post or reply that the account holder replied to.
- Quoting Post Author: The unique system-generated author ID for the Threads post or reply that the account holder quoted.
- Quoting ID:The unique system-generated ID for the Threads post or reply that the account holder quoted.
- Reposting Author ID: The unique system-generated author ID for the Threads post or reply that the account holder reposted.
- Reposting ID: The unique system-generated ID for the Threads post or reply that the account holder reposted.
- Responses in the Threads App may not be presented in chronological order.
- There are 4 types of data output scenarios: When the target creates a Thread, responds to a Thread, reposts a Thread, and quotes a Thread.
- There are no distinct markers denoting the initiation of a new Thread. To pinpoint the start of a new Thread, you must navigate through the data output and locate the section(s) where only "Post Author ID" and "Post Content ID" are present.
Meta Platforms Business Record Page 338
- To follow the thread conversation, the reader must locate the Post Content ID of the previous reply's post to accurately identify the response to the prior message. To find the preceding response, select the text you wish to find, use Ctrl+C (Copy) and Ctrl+F (Control Find) to locate the matching "Reply to (Post) ID" associated with the Post Content ID.
- When the user quoted a Thread, the data output will include the “Quoting Post Author” and “ Quoting ID.”
- When the user reposted a Thread, the data output will include the “Reposting Author ID” and “Reposting ID.”
Threads Posts And Replies

Threads Archived Stories Definition
Threads Archived Stories: Thread stories that the account holder crossposted to other platforms. Based on the account holder’s privacy setting in other platforms, the Thread stories may be archived.
Story ID: The unique system-generated ID associated with the Thread crossposting.
Timestamp: The date and time the Thread was crossposted by the account holder.
Photo ID: The unique system-generated ID associated with the photo.
Threads Archived Stories
No responsive records located
Community Notes Definition
Community Notes: Limited context to public content on the platform added by an account holder.
Content ID: The unique system generated ID of the content the account holder is making the note on.
Note ID: The unique system generated ID of the note made by the account holder.
Time: The date and timestamp of when the note was posted.
Note: The content of the note made by the account holder.
Note Visible: True/False
- True: The note is visible to users.
- False: The note is not visible to users.
URL: A list of URLs entered by the account holder as references supporting the claim of the note.
Community Notes

Threads Community Notes: Limited context to public content on the platform added by an account holder.
Content ID: The unique system generated ID of the content the account holder is making the note on.
Meta Platforms Business Record Page 339
Note ID: The unique system generated ID of the note made by the account holder.
Time: The date and timestamp of when the note was posted.
Note: The content of the note made by the account holder.
Note Visible: True/False
- True: The note is visible to users.
- False: The note is not visible to users.

Archived Quicksnap Definition
Archived Quicksnap: Displays media the account holder posted to their profile quicksnap that has been archived.
Quicksnap ID: Unique system generated identifier of the Quicksnap.
Timestamp: Date and timestamp the media was uploaded.
Recipients: The Account holders that received the media.
Owner: Owner of the account.
Author: The authorized account holder who uploaded the quicksnap.
- Privacy Setting: Displays the current privacy settings for the media.
Public: The privacy setting of the media is Public.
Private: The privacy setting of the media is Private.
Close Friends: The privacy setting of the media is only viewable to Close Friends.
- Reactions:
Reaction Emoji: The emoji used to react to the Quicksnap.
Archived Quicksnap
Meta Platforms Business Record Page 340
No responsive records located
Unarchived Stories Definition
Unarchived Stories: Displays media the user posted to their profile story that is not archived at the time of production.
Story ID: Unique system generated identifier of the story.
Time: Date and timestamp the media was uploaded.
Owner: Owner of the account.
Author: The authorized account holder who uploaded the story.
Bytes: Link to the media.
Privacy Setting: Displays current privacy settings for content.
- Public: The privacy setting of the content is Public.
- Private: The privacy setting of the content is Private.
- Close Friends: The privacy setting of the content is only viewable to Close Friends.
AI: Identifies if content was generated using AI
- True = Content was generated using AI
- False = Content was not generated AI
AI Searches: Searches made by the account holder that generate AI stickers within a story.
Unarchived Stories
No responsive records located
Shared Access Definition
Shared Access: The Instagram accounts the target has access to.
Shared Access Account: The account that was authorized to act on behalf of the shared account.
Action:
- Revoked Access: The account owner revokes someone's access to the shared account.
- Messaging Control Enabled: The account owner allows messaging control for the shared account.
Meta Platforms Business Record Page 341
- Accepted Invitation: The invitee accepts an invitation to access the shared account.
- Invitation Sent: The account owner sends an invitation to someone to access the shared account.
- Messaging Control Disabled: The account owner disables messaging control for the shared account.
- Invitation Expired: The system automatically expires an invitation to access the shared account.
- Cancelled Invitation: The account owner cancels an invitation to access the shared account.
- Invitation Declined: The invitee declines an invitation to access the shared account.
Time: The date and timestamp when the shared account performed an action.
Account Owner: The account owner that authorizes shared access.
Shared Access
No responsive records located
Last Location Area Definition
Last Location Area: Within an area of 10,000 people or 2 square kilometers, whichever is smaller. For population centers less than 10,000 people, the accuracy is within 500 kilometers.
Timestamp: Date and time of the last location area.
Latitude: Latitude associated with the last location area.
Longitude: Longitude associated with the last location area.
